<h3>In the show running-config command, which part of the syntax is represented by running-config ?</h3>
<ul>
<li>the command</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">a keyword</span></li>
<li>a variable</li>
<li>a prompt<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<div class="itemfeedback"><span class="mattext">The first part of the syntax, <b>show </b>, is the command, and the second part of the syntax, <b>running-config, </b>is the keyword. The keyword specifies what should be displayed as the output of the <b>show </b>command.</span></div>
<div class="remediation"></div>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>An employee at a branch office is creating a quote for a customer. In order to do this, the employee needs to access confidential pricing information from internal servers at the Head Office. What type of network would the employee access?</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">an intranet</span></li>
<li>the Internet</li>
<li>an extranet</li>
<li>a local area network<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Intranet is a term used to refer to a private connection of LANs and WANs that belongs to an organization. An intranet is designed to be accessible only by the organization&#8217;s members, employees, or others with authorization.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which statement describes the use of powerline networking technology?</h3>
<ul>
<li>New &#8220;smart&#8221; electrical cabling is used to extend an existing home LAN.</li>
<li>A home LAN is installed without the use of physical cabling.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">A device connects to an existing home LAN using an adapter and an existing electrical outlet.</span></li>
<li>Wireless access points use powerline adapters to distribute data  through the home LAN.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Powerline networking adds the ability to connect a device to the network using an adapter wherever there is an electrical outlet.​ The network uses existing electrical wiring to send data. It is not a replacement for physical cabling, but it can add functionality in places where wireless access points cannot be used or cannot reach devices.​</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>

<h3>A networking technician is working on the wireless network at a medical clinic. The technician accidentally sets up the wireless network so that patients can see the medical records data of other patients. Which of the four network characteristics has been violated in this situation?</h3>
<ul>
<li>fault tolerance</li>
<li>scalability</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">security</span></li>
<li>Quality of Service (QoS)</li>
<li>reliability<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Network security includes protecting the confidentiality of data that is on the network. In this case, because confidential data has been made available to unauthorized users, the security characteristic of the network has failed.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3>Match each characteristic to its corresponding Internet connectivity type. (Not all options are used.)</h3>
<figure id="attachment_197" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-197" style="width: 2029px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-002-1-1024x341.jpg 1024w, https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-002-1-768x256.jpg 768w, <table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>DSL is an always-on, high bandwidth connection that runs over telephone lines. Cable uses the same coaxial cable that carries television signals into the home to provide Internet access. Dialup telephone is much slower than either DSL or cable, but is the least expensive option for home users because it can use any telephone line and a simple modem. Satellite requires a clear line of sight and is affected by trees and other obstructions. None of these typical home options use dedicated leased lines such as T1/E1 and T3/E3.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>

<h3>What two criteria are used to help select a network medium from various network media? (Choose two.)</h3>
<ul>
<li>the types of data that need to be prioritized</li>
<li>the cost of the end devices utilized in the network</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">the distance the selected medium can successfully carry a signal</span></li>
<li>the number of intermediate devices installed in the network</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">the environment where the selected medium is to be installed</span><br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Criteria for choosing a network medium are the distance the selected medium can successfully carry a signal, the environment in which the selected medium is to be installed, the amount of data and the speed at which the data must be transmitted, and the cost of the medium and its installation.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>

<li>
<h3>What type of network traffic requires QoS?</h3>
<ul>
<li>email</li>
<li>on-line purchasing</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">video conferencing</span></li>
<li>wiki<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Video conferencing utilizes real-time audio and video communications. Both of these are time-sensitive and bandwidth-intensive forms of communication that require quality of service to be active on the network. QoS will ensure an uninterrupted user experience.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>

<li>
<h3>A user is implementing security on a small office network. Which two actions would provide the minimum security requirements for this network? (Choose two.)</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">implementing a firewall</span></li>
<li>installing a wireless network</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">installing antivirus software</span></li>
<li>implementing an intrusion detection system</li>
<li>adding a dedicated intrusion prevention device<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Technically complex security measures such as intrusion prevention and intrusion prevention systems are usually associated with business networks rather than home networks. Installing antivirus software, antimalware software, and implementing a firewall will usually be the minimum requirements for home networks. Installing a home wireless network will not improve network security, and will require further security actions to be taken.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>

<h3>Passwords can be used to restrict access to all or parts of the Cisco IOS. Select the modes and interfaces that can be protected with passwords. (Choose three.)</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">VTY interface </span></li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">console interface</span></li>
<li>Ethernet interface</li>
<li>boot IOS mode</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">privileged EXEC mode</span></li>
<li>router configuration mode<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Access to the VTY and console interfaces can be restricted using passwords. Out-of-band management of the router can be restricted in both user EXEC and privileged EXEC modes.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li>the AUX interface</li>

<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">the switch virtual interface</span></li>
<li>the first Ethernet port interface<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>In a Layer 2 switch, there is a switch virtual interface (SVI) that provides a means for remotely managing the device.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>

<h3>What function does pressing the Tab key have when entering a command in IOS?</h3>
<ul>
<li>It aborts the current command and returns to configuration mode.</li>
<li>It exits configuration mode and returns to user EXEC mode.</li>
<li>It moves the cursor to the beginning of the next line.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">It completes the remainder of a partially typed word in a command.</span><br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Pressing the Tab key after a command has been partially typed will cause the IOS to complete the rest of the command.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>

<li>
<h3>While trying to solve a network issue, a technician made multiple changes to the current router configuration file. The changes did not solve the problem and were not saved. What action can the technician take to discard the changes and work with the file in NVRAM?</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">Issue the reload command without saving the running configuration.</span></li>
<li>Delete the vlan.dat file and reboot the device.</li>
<li>Close and reopen the terminal emulation software.</li>
<li>Issue the copy startup-config running-config command.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The technician does not want to make any mistakes trying to remove all the changes that were done to the running configuration file. The solution is to reboot the router without saving the running configuration. The copy startup-config running-config command does not overwrite the running configuration file with the configuration file stored in NVRAM, but rather it just has an additive effect.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>An administrator uses the Ctrl-Shift-6 key combination on a switch after issuing the ping command. What is the purpose of using these keystrokes?</h3>
<ul>
<li>to restart the ping process</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">to interrupt the ping process</span></li>
<li>to exit to a different configuration mode</li>
<li>to allow the user to complete the command<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>To interrupt an IOS process such as ping or traceroute , a user enters the Ctrl-Shift-6 key combination. Tab completes the remainder of parameters or arguments within a command. To exit from configuration mode to privileged mode use the Ctrl-Z keystroke. CTRL-R will redisplay the line just typed, thus making it easier for the user to press Enter and reissue the ping command.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Refer to the exhibit. A network administrator is configuring access control to switch SW1. If the administrator uses a console connection to connect to the switch, which password is needed to access user EXEC mode?</h3>
<figure id="attachment_194" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-194" style="width: 487px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-194" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20487%20235'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 1 – 3 Basic Network Connectivity and Communications Exam Answers 02" width="487" height="235" data-lazy-src="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-02.gif" /><noscript><img decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-194" src="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-02.gif" alt="CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 1 – 3 Basic Network Connectivity and Communications Exam Answers 02" width="487" height="235" /></noscript><figcaption id="caption-attachment-194" class="wp-caption-text">CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 1 – 3 Basic Network Connectivity and Communications Exam Answers 02</figcaption></figure>
<ul>
<li>letmein</li>
<li>secretin</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">lineconin</span></li>
<li>linevtyin<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Telnet accesses a network device through the virtual interface configured with the line VTY command. The password configured under this is required to access the user EXEC mode. The password configured under the line console 0 command is required to gain entry through the console port, and the enable and enable secret passwords are used to allow entry into the privileged EXEC mode.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>

<h3>A technician configures a switch with these commands:</h3>
<p><span style="font-family: 'courier new', courier, monospace;">SwitchA(config)# interface vlan 1 </span><br />
<span style="font-family: 'courier new', courier, monospace;">SwitchA(config-if)# ip address 192.168.1.1 255.255.255.0 </span><br />
<span style="font-family: 'courier new', courier, monospace;">SwitchA(config-if)# no shutdown</span></p>
<h3>What is the technician configuring?</h3>
<ul>
<li>Telnet access</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">SVI</span></li>
<li>password encryption</li>
<li>physical switchport access<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>For a switch to have an IP address, a switch virtual interface must be configured. This allows the switch to be managed remotely over the network.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which command or key combination allows a user to return to the previous level in the command hierarchy?</h3>
<ul>
<li>end</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">exit</span></li>
<li>Ctrl-Z</li>
<li>Ctrl-C<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>End and CTRL-Z return the user to the privileged EXEC mode. Ctrl-C ends a command in process. The exit command returns the user to the previous level.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What are two characteristics of RAM on a Cisco device? (Choose two.)</h3>
<ul>
<li>RAM provides nonvolatile storage.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">The configuration that is actively running on the device is stored in RAM. </span></li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">The contents of RAM are lost during a power cycle.</span></li>
<li>RAM is a component in Cisco switches but not in Cisco routers.</li>
<li>RAM is able to store multiple versions of IOS and configuration files.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>RAM stores data that is used by the device to support network operations. The running configuration is stored in RAM. This type of memory is considered volatile memory because data is lost during a power cycle. Flash memory stores the IOS and delivers a copy of the IOS into RAM when a device is powered on. Flash memory is nonvolatile since it retains stored contents during a loss of power.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which two host names follow the guidelines for naming conventions on Cisco IOS devices? (Choose two.)</h3>
<ul>
<li>Branch2!</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">RM-3-Switch-2A4</span></li>
<li>Floor(15)</li>
<li>HO Floor 17</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">SwBranch799</span><br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Some guidelines for naming conventions are that names should:Start with a letter<br />
Contain no spaces<br />
End with a letter or digit<br />
Use only letters, digits, and dashes<br />
Be less than 64 characters in length</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>How is SSH different from Telnet?</h3>
<ul>
<li>SSH makes connections over the network, whereas Telnet is for out-of-band access.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">SSH provides security to remote sessions by encrypting messages and using user authentication. Telnet is considered insecure and sends messages in plaintext.</span></li>
<li>SSH requires the use of the PuTTY terminal emulation program. Tera Term must be used to connect to devices through the use of Telnet.</li>
<li>SSH must be configured over an active network connection, whereas Telnet is used to connect to a device from a console connection.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>SSH is the preferred protocol for connecting to a device operating system over the network because it is much more secure than Telnet. Both SSH and Telnet are used to connect to devices over the network, and so are both used in-band. PuTTY and Terra Term can be used to make both SSH and Telnet connections.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>An administrator is configuring a switch console port with a password. In what order will the administrator travel through the IOS modes of operation in order to reach the mode in which the configuration commands will be entered? (Not all options are used.)</h3>

Network Connectivity and Communications Exam Answers 003" width="2019" height="838" https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-003-1-300x125.jpg 300w, https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-003-1-768x319.jpg 768w, https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-003-1-1536x638.jpg 1536w" sizes="(max-width: 2019px) 100vw, 2019px" /></noscript></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-198" class="wp-caption-text">CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 1 – 3 Basic Network Connectivity and Communications Exam Answers 003</figcaption></figure>
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The configuration mode that the administrator first encounters is user EXEC mode. After the <b>enable </b>command is entered, the next mode is privileged EXEC mode. From there, the<b> configure termina</b>l command is entered to move to global configuration mode. Finally, the administrator enters the<b> line console 0 </b>command to enter the mode in which the configuration will be entered.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What are three characteristics of an SVI? (Choose three.)</h3>
<ul>
<li>It is designed as a security protocol to protect switch ports.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">It is not associated with any physical interface on a switch.</span></li>
<li>It is a special interface that allows connectivity by different types of media.</li>
<li>It is required to allow connectivity by any device at any location.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">It provides a means to remotely manage a switch. </span></li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">It is associated with VLAN1 by default.</span><br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Switches have one or more switch virtual interfaces (SVIs). SVIs are created in software since there is no physical hardware associated with them. Virtual interfaces provide a means to remotely manage a switch over a network that is using IP. Each switch comes with one SVI appearing in the default configuration &#8220;out-of-the-box.&#8221; The default SVI interface is VLAN1.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What command is used to verify the condition of the switch interfaces, including the status of the interfaces and a configured IP address?</h3>
<ul>
<li>ipconfig</li>
<li>ping</li>
<li>traceroute</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">show ip interface brief</span><br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The show ip interface brief command is used to display a brief synopsis of the condition of the device interfaces. The ipconfig command is used to verify TCP/IP properties on a host. The ping command is used to verify Layer 3 connectivity. The traceroute command is used to trace the network path from source to destination.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>

<h3>In the show running-config command, which part of the syntax is represented by running-config?</h3>
<ul>
<li>the command</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">a keyword</span></li>
<li>a variable</li>
<li>a prompt<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The first part of the syntax, show , is the command, and the second part of the syntax, running-config, is the keyword. The keyword specifies what should be displayed as the output of the show command.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>After making configuration changes on a Cisco switch, a network administrator issues a copy running-config startup-config command. What is the result of issuing this command?</h3>
<ul>
<li>The new configuration will be stored in flash memory.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">The new configuration will be loaded if the switch is restarted.</span></li>
<li>The current IOS file will be replaced with the newly configured file.</li>
<li>The configuration changes will be removed and the original configuration will be restored.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>With the copy running-config startup-config command, the content of the current operating configuration replaces the startup configuration file stored in NVRAM. The configuration file saved in NVRAM will be loaded when the device is restarted.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What command will prevent all unencrypted passwords from displaying in plain text in a configuration file?</h3>
<ul>
<li>(config)# enable password secret</li>
<li>(config)# enable secret Secret_Password</li>
<li>(config-line)# password secret</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">(config)# service password-encryption</span></li>
<li>(config)# enable secret Encrypted_Password<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>To prevent all configured passwords from appearing in plain text in configuration files, an administrator can execute the service password-encryption command. This command encrypts all configured passwords in the configuration file.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>A network administrator enters the service password-encryption command into the configuration mode of a router. What does this command accomplish?</h3>
<ul>
<li>This command encrypts passwords as they are transmitted across serial WAN links.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">This command prevents someone from viewing the running configuration passwords.</span></li>
<li>This command enables a strong encryption algorithm for the enable secret password command.</li>
<li>This command automatically encrypts passwords in configuration files that are currently stored in NVRAM.</li>
<li>This command provides an exclusive encrypted password for external service personnel who are required to do router maintenance.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The startup-config and running-config files display most passwords in plaintext. Use the service password-encryption global config command to encrypt all plaintext passwords in these files.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What method can be used by two computers to ensure that packets are not dropped because too much data is being sent too quickly?</h3>
<ul>
<li>encapsulation</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">flow control</span></li>
<li>access method</li>
<li>response timeout<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>In order for two computers to be able to communicate effectively, there must be a mechanism that allows both the source and destination to set the timing of the transmission and receipt of data. Flow control allows for this by ensuring that data is not sent too fast for it to be received properly.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which statement accurately describes a TCP/IP encapsulation process when a PC is sending data to the network?</h3>
<ul>
<li>Data is sent from the internet layer to the network access layer.</li>
<li>Packets are sent from the network access layer to the transport layer.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">Segments are sent from the transport layer to the internet layer.</span></li>
<li>Frames are sent from the network access layer to the internet layer.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>When the data is traveling from the PC to the network, the transport layer sends segments to the internet layer. The internet layer sends packets to the network access layer, which creates frames and then converts the frames to bits. The bits are released to the network media.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What three application layer protocols are part of the TCP/IP protocol suite? (Choose three.)</h3>
<ul>
<li>ARP</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">DHCP </span></li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">DNS </span></li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">FTP</span></li>
<li>NAT</li>
<li>PPP<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>DNS, DHCP, and FTP are all application layer protocols in the TCP/IP protocol suite. ARP and PPP are network access layer protocols, and NAT is an internet layer protocol in the TCP/IP protocol suite.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Match the description to the organization. (Not all options are used.)</h3>

<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The EIA is an international standards and trade organization for electronics organizations. It is best known for its standards related to electrical wiring, connectors, and the 19-inch racks used to mount networking equipment.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which name is assigned to the transport layer PDU?</h3>
<ul>
<li>bits</li>
<li>data</li>
<li>frame</li>
<li>packet</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">segment</span><br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Application data is passed down the protocol stack on its way to be transmitted across the network media. During the process, various protocols add information to it at each level. At each stage of the process, a PDU (protocol data unit) has a different name to reflect its new functions. The PDUs are named according to the protocols of the TCP/IP suite: Data &#8211; The general term for the PDU used at the application layer.<br />
Segment &#8211; transport layer PDU<br />
Packet &#8211; network layer PDU<br />
Frame – data link layer PDU<br />
Bits &#8211; A physical layer PDU used when physically transmitting data over the medium</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>When IPv4 addressing is manually configured on a web server, which property of the IPv4 configuration identifies the network and host portion for an IPv4 address?</h3>
<ul>
<li>DNS server address</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">subnet mask</span></li>
<li>default gateway</li>
<li>DHCP server address<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>There are several components that need to be entered when configuring IPv4 for an end device: IPv4 address &#8211; uniquely identifies an end device on the network<br />
Subnet mask &#8211; determines the network address portion and host portion for an IPv4 address<br />
Default gateway &#8211; the IP address of the router interface used for communicating with hosts in another network<br />
DNS server addres s &#8211; the IP address of the Domain Name System (DNS) server<br />
DHCP server address (if DHCP is used) is not configured manually on end devices. It will be provided by a DHCP server when an end device requests an IP address.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What process involves placing one PDU inside of another PDU?</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">encapsulation</span></li>
<li>encoding</li>
<li>segmentation</li>
<li>flow control<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>When a message is placed inside of another message, this is known as encapsulation. On networks, encapsulation takes place when one protocol data unit is carried inside of the data field of the next lower protocol data unit.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What layer is responsible for routing messages through an internetwork in the TCP/IP model?</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">internet</span></li>
<li>transport</li>
<li>network access</li>
<li>session<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The TCP/IP model consists of four layers: application, transport, internet, and network access. Of these four layers, it is the internet layer that is responsible for routing messages. The session layer is not part of the TCP/IP model but is rather part of the OSI model.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>

<li>
<h3>Which PDU format is used when bits are received from the network medium by the NIC of a host?</h3>
<ul>
<li>file</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">frame</span></li>
<li>packet</li>
<li>segment<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>When received at the physical layer of a host, the bits are formatted into a frame at the data link layer. A packet is the PDU at the network layer. A segment is the PDU at the transport layer. A file is a data structure that may be used at the application layer.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Refer to the exhibit. ServerB is attempting to contact HostA. Which two statements correctly identify the addressing that ServerB will generate in the process? (Choose two.)</h3>
<figure id="attachment_195" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-195" style="width: 392px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-195" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20392%20320'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 1 – 3 Basic Network Connectivity and Communications Exam Answers 03" width="392" height="320" data-lazy-srcset="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-03-1.jpg 392w, https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-03-1-300x245.jpg 300w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 392px) 100vw, 392px" data-lazy-src="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-03-1.jpg" /><noscript><img decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-195" src="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-03-1.jpg" alt="CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 1 – 3 Basic Network Connectivity and Communications Exam Answers 03" width="392" height="320" srcset="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-03-1.jpg 392w, https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-03-1-300x245.jpg 300w" sizes="(max-width: 392px) 100vw, 392px" /></noscript><figcaption id="caption-attachment-195" class="wp-caption-text">CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 1 – 3 Basic Network Connectivity and Communications Exam Answers 03</figcaption></figure>
<ul>
<li>ServerB will generate a packet with the destination IP address of RouterB.</li>
<li>ServerB will generate a frame with the destination MAC address of SwitchB.</li>
<li>ServerB will generate a packet with the destination IP address of RouterA.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">ServerB will generate a frame with the destination MAC address of RouterB. </span></li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">ServerB will generate a packet with the destination IP address of HostA.</span></li>
<li>ServerB will generate a frame with the destination MAC address of RouterA.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>In order to send data to HostA, ServerB will generate a packet that contains the IP address of the destination device on the remote network and a frame that contains the MAC address of the default gateway device on the local network.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>

<h3>Which method allows a computer to react accordingly when it requests data from a server and the server takes too long to respond?</h3>
<ul>
<li>encapsulation</li>
<li>flow control</li>
<li>access method</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">response timeout </span><br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>If a computer makes a request and does not hear a response within an acceptable amount of time, the computer assumes that no answer is coming and reacts accordingly.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>A web client is receiving a response for a web page from a web server. From the perspective of the client, what is the correct order of the protocol stack that is used to decode the received transmission?</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">Ethernet, IP, TCP, HTTP</span></li>
<li>HTTP, TCP, IP, Ethernet</li>
<li>Ethernet, TCP, IP, HTTP</li>
<li>HTTP, Ethernet, IP, TCP<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>1. HTTP governs the way that a web server and client interact.<br />
2. TCP manages individual conversations between web servers and clients.<br />
3. IP is responsible for delivery across the best path to the destination.<br />
4. Ethernet takes the packet from IP and formats it for transmission.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which two OSI model layers have the same functionality as a single layer of the TCP/IP model? (Choose two.)</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">data link</span></li>
<li>network</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">physical</span></li>
<li>session</li>
<li>transport<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The OSI data link and physical layers together are equivalent to the TCP/IP network access layer. The OSI transport layer is functionally equivalent to the TCP/IP transport layer, and the OSI network layer is equivalent to the TCP/IP internet layer. The OSI application, presentation, and session layers are functionally equivalent to the application layer within the TCP/IP model.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>At which layer of the OSI model would a logical address be added during encapsulation?</h3>
<ul>
<li>physical layer</li>
<li>data link layer</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">network layer</span></li>
<li>transport layer<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Logical addresses, also known as IP addresses, are added at the network layer. Physical addresses are edded at the data link layer. Port addresses are added at the transport layer. No addresses are added at the physical layer.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What is a characteristic of multicast messages?</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">They are sent to a select group of hosts.</span></li>
<li>They are sent to all hosts on a network.</li>
<li>They must be acknowledged.</li>
<li>They are sent to a single destination.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Multicast is a one-to-many type of communication. Multicast messages are addressed to a specific multicast group.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which statement is correct about network protocols?</h3>
<ul>
<li>Network protocols define the type of hardware that is used and how it is mounted in racks.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">They define how messages are exchanged between the source and the destination.</span></li>
<li>They all function in the network access layer of TCP/IP.</li>
<li>They are only required for exchange of messages between devices on remote networks.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Network protocols are implemented in hardware, or software, or both. They interact with each other within different layers of a protocol stack. Protocols have nothing to do with the installation of the network equipment. Network protocols are required to exchange information between source and destination devices in both local and remote networks.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What is an advantage of network devices using open standard protocols?</h3>
<ul>
<li>Network communications is confined to data transfers between devices from the same vendor.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">A client host and a server running different operating systems can successfully exchange data.</span></li>
<li>Internet access can be controlled by a single ISP in each market.</li>
<li>Competition and innovation are limited to specific types of products.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>An advantage of network devices implementing open standard protocols, such as from the TCP/IP suite, is that clients and servers running different operating systems can communicate with each other. Open standard protocols facilitate innovation and competition between vendors and across markets, and can reduce the occurrence of monopolies in networking markets.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which device performs the function of determining the path that messages should take through internetworks?</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">a router</span></li>
<li>a firewall</li>
<li>a web server</li>
<li>a DSL modem<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>A router is used to determine the path that the messages should take through the network. A firewall is used to filter incoming and outgoing traffic. A DSL modem is used to provide Internet connection for a home or an organization.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>

<h3>Open the PT Activity. Perform the tasks in the activity instructions and then answer the question.</h3>
<h3>What is the IP address of the switch virtual interface (SVI) on Switch0?</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">192.168.5.10</span></li>
<li>192.168.10.5</li>
<li>192.168.10.1</li>
<li>192.168.5.0<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>After the enable command is issued, the show running-configuration command or the show ip interfaces brief command will display the IP address of the switch virtual interface (SVI).</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>

<li>
<h3>Why would a Layer 2 switch need an IP address?</h3>
<ul>
<li>to enable the switch to send broadcast frames to attached PCs</li>
<li>to enable the switch to function as a default gateway</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">to enable the switch to be managed remotely</span></li>
<li>to enable the switch to receive frames from attached PCs<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>A switch, as a Layer 2 device, does not need an IP address to transmit frames to attached devices. However, when a switch is accessed remotely through the network, it must have a Layer 3 address. The IP address must be applied to a virtual interface rather than to a physical interface. Routers, not switches, function as default gateways.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>

<h3>Refer to the exhibit. An administrator is trying to configure the switch but receives the error message that is displayed in the exhibit. What is the problem?</h3>
<figure id="attachment_193" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-193" style="width: 308px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-193" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20308%2055'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 1 – 3 Basic Network Connectivity and Communications Exam Answers 01" width="308" height="55" data-lazy-srcset="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-01.png 308w, https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-01-300x54.png 300w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 308px) 100vw, 308px" data-lazy-src="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-01.png" /><noscript><img decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-193" src="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-01.png" alt="CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 1 – 3 Basic Network Connectivity and Communications Exam Answers 01" width="308" height="55" srcset="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-01.png 308w, https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-1-–-3-Basic-Network-Connectivity-and-Communications-Exam-Answers-01-300x54.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 308px) 100vw, 308px" /></noscript><figcaption id="caption-attachment-193" class="wp-caption-text">CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 1 – 3 Basic Network Connectivity and Communications Exam Answers 01</figcaption></figure>
<ul>
<li>The entire command, configure terminal, must be used.</li>
<li>The administrator is already in global configuration mode.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">The administrator must first enter privileged EXEC mode before issuing the command.</span></li>
<li>The administrator must connect via the console port to access global configuration mode.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>In order to enter global configuration mode, the command configure terminal , or a shortened version such as config t , must be entered from privileged EXEC mode. In this scenario the administrator is in user EXEC mode, as indicated by the &gt; symbol after the hostname. The administrator would need to use the enable command to move into privileged EXEC mode before entering the configure terminal command.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>

<li>presentation layer</li>
</ul>

A network administrator is measuring the transfer of bits across the company backbone for a mission critical financial application. The administrator notices that the network throughput appears lower than the bandwidth expected. Which three factors could influence the differences in throughput? (Choose three.)</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">the amount of traffic that is currently crossing the network</span></li>
<li>the sophistication of the encapsulation method applied to the data</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">the type of traffic that is crossing the network </span></li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">the latency that is created by the number of network devices that the data is crossing</span></li>
<li>the bandwidth of the WAN connection to the Internet</li>
<li>the reliability of the gigabit Ethernet infrastructure of the backbone<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Throughput usually does not match the specified bandwidth of physical links due to multiple factors. These factors include, the amount of traffic, type of traffic, and latency created by the network devices the data has to cross.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What are two characteristics of fiber-optic cable? (Choose two.)</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">It is not affected by EMI or RFI.</span></li>
<li>Each pair of cables is wrapped in metallic foil.</li>
<li>It combines the technique of cancellation, shielding, and twisting to protect data.</li>
<li>It typically contains 4 pairs of fiber-optic wires.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">It is more expensive than UTP cabling is.</span><br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Fiber-optic cabling supports higher bandwidth than UTP for longer distances. Fiber is immune to EMI and RFI, but costs more, requires more skill to install, and requires more safety precautions.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What is a primary role of the Physical layer in transmitting data on the network?</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">create the signals that represent the bits in each frame on to the media</span></li>
<li>provide physical addressing to the devices</li>
<li>determine the path packets take through the network</li>
<li>control data access to the media<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The OSI physical layer provides the means to transport the bits that make up a frame across the network media. This layer accepts a complete frame from the data link layer and encodes it as a series of signals that are transmitted to the local media.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>

<li>
<h3>With the use of unshielded twisted-pair copper wire in a network, what causes crosstalk within the cable pairs?</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">the magnetic field around the adjacent pairs of wire</span></li>
<li>the use of braided wire to shield the adjacent wire pairs</li>
<li>the reflection of the electrical wave back from the far end of the cable</li>
<li>the collision caused by two nodes trying to use the media simultaneously<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Crosstalk is a type of noise, or interference that occurs when signal transmission on one wire interferes with another wire. When current flows through a wire a magnetic field is produced. The produced magnetic field will interface the signal carried in the adjacent wire.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Refer to the graphic. What type of cabling is shown?</h3>
<figure id="attachment_209" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-209" style="width: 198px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-209" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20198%20157'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 4 – 7 Ethernet Concepts Exam Answers 01" width="198" height="157" data-lazy-src="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-4-–-7-Ethernet-Concepts-Exam-Answers-01-1.jpg" /><noscript><img decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-209" src="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-4-–-7-Ethernet-Concepts-Exam-Answers-01-1.jpg" alt="CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 4 – 7 Ethernet Concepts Exam Answers 01" width="198" height="157" /></noscript><figcaption id="caption-attachment-209" class="wp-caption-text">CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 4 – 7 Ethernet Concepts Exam Answers 01</figcaption></figure>
<ul>
<li>STP</li>
<li>UTP</li>
<li>coax</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">fiber</span><br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Network cabling include different types of cables:<br />
UTP cable consists of four pairs of color-coded wires that have been twisted together and then encased in a flexible plastic sheath.<br />
STP cable uses four pairs of wires, each wrapped in a foil shield, which are then wrapped in an overall metallic braid or foil.<br />
Coaxial cable uses a copper conductor and a layer of flexible plastic insulation surrounds the copper conductor.<br />
Fiber cable is a flexible, extremely thin, transparent strand of glass surrounded by plastic insulation.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>In addition to the cable length, what two factors could interfere with the communication carried over UTP cables? (Choose two.)</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">crosstalk</span></li>
<li>bandwidth</li>
<li>size of the network</li>
<li>signal modulation technique</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">electromagnetic interference</span><br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Copper media is widely used in network communications. However, copper media is limited by distance and signal interference. Data is transmitted on copper cables as electrical pulses. The electrical pulses are susceptible to interference from two sources:<br />
Electromagnetic interference (EMI) or radio frequency interference (RFI) &#8211; EMI and RFI signals can distort and corrupt the data signals being carried by copper media.<br />
Crosstalk &#8211; Crosstalk is a disturbance caused by the electric or magnetic fields of a signal on one wire interfering with the signal in an adjacent wire.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>

<h3>Which two devices commonly affect wireless networks? (Choose two.)</h3>
<ul>
<li>Blu-ray players</li>
<li>home theaters</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">cordless phones </span></li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">microwaves</span></li>
<li>incandescent light bulbs</li>
<li>external hard drives<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Radio Frequency Interference (RFI) is the interference that is caused by radio transmitters and other devices that are transmitting in the same frequency.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which two statements describe the services provided by the data link layer? (Choose two.)</h3>
<ul>
<li>It defines the end-to-end delivery addressing scheme.</li>
<li>It maintains the path between the source and destination devices during the data transmission.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">It manages the access of frames to the network media.</span></li>
<li>It provides reliable delivery through link establishment and flow control.</li>
<li>It ensures that application data will be transmitted according to the prioritization.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">It packages various Layer 3 PDUs into a frame format that is compatible with the network interface.</span><br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The data link layer is divided into two sub layers, namely Logical Link Control (LLC) and Media Access Control (MAC). LLC forms a frame from the network layer PDU into a format that conforms to the requirements of the network interface and media. A network layer PDU might be for IPv4 or IPv6. The MAC sub layer defines the media access processes performed by the hardware. It manages the frame access to the network media according to the physical signaling requirements (copper cable, fiber optic, wireless, etc.)</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What is the function of the CRC value that is found in the FCS field of a frame?</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">to verify the integrity of the received frame</span></li>
<li>to verify the physical address in the frame</li>
<li>to verify the logical address in the frame</li>
<li>to compute the checksum header for the data field in the frame<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The CRC value in the FCS field of the received frame is compared to the computed CRC value of that frame, in order to verify the integrity of the frame. If the two values do not match, then the frame is discarded.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What is contained in the trailer of a data-link frame?</h3>
<ul>
<li>logical address</li>
<li>physical address</li>
<li>data</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">error detection</span><br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The trailer in a data-link frame contains error detection information that is pertinent to the frame included in the FCS field. The header contains control information, such as the addressing, while the area that is indicated by the word &#8220;data&#8221; includes the data, transport layer PDU, and the IP header.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which statement describes a characteristic of the frame header fields of the data link layer?</h3>
<ul>
<li>They all include the flow control and logical connection fields.</li>
<li>Ethernet frame header fields contain Layer 3 source and destination addresses.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">They vary depending on protocols.</span></li>
<li>They include information on user applications.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>All data link layer protocols encapsulate the Layer 3 PDU within the data field of the frame. However, the structure of the frame and the fields that are contained in the header vary according to the protocol. Different data link layer protocols may use different fields, like priority/quality of service, logical connection control, physical link control, flow control, and congestion control.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>A network team is comparing physical WAN topologies for connecting remote sites to a headquarters building. Which topology provides high availability and connects some, but not all, remote sites?</h3>
<ul>
<li>mesh</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">partial mesh</span></li>
<li>hub and spoke</li>
<li>point-to-point<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Partial mesh topologies provide high availability by interconnecting multiple remote sites, but do not require a connection between all remote sites. A mesh topology requires point-to-point links with every system being connected to every other system. A point-to-point topology is where each device is connected to one other device. A hub and spoke uses a central device in a star topology that connects to other point-to-point devices.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which two fields or features does Ethernet examine to determine if a received frame is passed to the data link layer or discarded by the NIC? (Choose two.)</h3>
<ul>
<li>auto-MDIX</li>
<li>CEF</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">Frame Check Sequence </span></li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">minimum frame size</span></li>
<li>source MAC address<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>An Ethernet frame is not processed and is discarded if it is smaller than the minimum (64 bytes) or if the calculated frame check sequence (FCS) value does not match the received FCS value. Auto-MDIX (automatic medium-dependent interface crossover) is Layer 1 technology that detects cable straight-through or crossover types. The source MAC address is not used to determine how the frame is received. CEF (Cisco Express Forwarding) is a technology used to expedite Layer 3 switching.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which media communication type does not require media arbitration in the data link layer?</h3>
<ul>
<li>deterministic</li>
<li>half-duplex</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">full-duplex</span></li>
<li>controlled access<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Half-duplex communication occurs when both devices can both transmit and receive on the medium but cannot do so simultaneously. Full-duplex communication occurs when both devices can transmit and receive on the medium at the same time and therefore does not require media arbitration. Half-duplex communication is typically contention-based, whereas controlled (deterministic) access is applied in technologies where devices take turns to access the medium.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which statement describes an extended star topology?</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">End devices connect to a central intermediate device, which in turn connects to other central intermediate devices.</span></li>
<li>End devices are connected together by a bus and each bus connects to a central intermediate device.</li>
<li>Each end system is connected to its respective neighbor via an intermediate device.</li>
<li>All end and intermediate devices are connected in a chain to each other.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>In an extended star topology, central intermediate devices interconnect other star topologies.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What is a characteristic of the LLC sublayer?</h3>
<ul>
<li>It provides the logical addressing required that identifies the device.</li>
<li>It provides delimitation of data according to the physical signaling requirements of the medium.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">It places information in the frame allowing multiple Layer 3 protocols to use the same network interface and media.</span></li>
<li>It defines software processes that provide services to the physical layer.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The Logical Link Control (LLC) defines the software processes that provide services to the network layer protocols. The information is placed by LLC in the frame and identifies which network layer protocol is being used for the frame. This information allows multiple Layer 3 protocols, such as IPv4 and IPv6, to utilize the same network interface and media.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What are three ways that media access control is used in networking? (Choose three.)</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">Ethernet utilizes CSMA/CD.</span></li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">Media access control provides placement of data frames onto the media.</span></li>
<li>Contention-based access is also known as deterministic.</li>
<li>802.11 utilizes CSMA/CD.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">Data link layer protocols define the rules for access to different media.</span></li>
<li>Networks with controlled access have reduced performance due to data collisions.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Wired Ethernet networks use CSMA/CD for media access control. IEEE 802.11 wireless networks use CSMA/CA, a similar method. Media access control defines the way data frames get placed on the media. The controlled access method is deterministic, not a contention-based access to networks. Because each device has its own time to use the medium, controlled access networks such as legacy Token Ring do not have collisions.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>During the encapsulation process, what occurs at the data link layer for a PC connected to an Ethernet network?</h3>
<ul>
<li>An IP address is added.</li>
<li>The logical address is added.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">The physical address is added.</span></li>
<li>The process port number is added.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The Ethernet frame includes the source and destination physical address. The trailer includes a CRC value in the Frame Check Sequence field to allow the receiving device to determine if the frame has been changed (has errors) during the transmission.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What three items are contained in an Ethernet header and trailer? (Choose three.)</h3>
<ul>
<li>source IP address</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">source MAC address</span></li>
<li>destination IP address</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">destination MAC address </span></li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">error-checking information</span><br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Layer 2 headers contain the following:Frame start and stop indicator flags at the beginning and end of a frame<br />
Addressing &#8211; for Ethernet networks this part of the header contains source and destination MAC addresses<br />
Type field to indicate what Layer 3 protocol is being used<br />
Error detection to determine if the frame arrived without error</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What type of communication rule would best describe CSMA/CD?</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">access method</span></li>
<li>flow control</li>
<li>message encapsulation</li>
<li>message encoding<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Carrier sense multiple access collision detection (CSMA/CD) is the access method used with Ethernet. The access method rule of communication dictates how a network device is able to place a signal on the carrier. CSMA/CD dictates those rules on an Ethernet network and CSMA/CA dictates those rules on an 802.11 wireless LAN.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which three basic parts are common to all frame types supported by the data link layer? (Choose three.)</h3>
<ul>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">header</span></li>
<li>type field</li>
<li>MTU size</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">data </span></li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">trailer</span></li>
<li>CRC value<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The data link protocol is responsible for NIC-to-NIC communications within the same network. Although there are many different data link layer protocols that describe data link layer frames, each frame type has three basic parts:<br />
Header<br />
Data<br />
Trailer</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Which statement is true about the CSMA/CD access method that is used in Ethernet?</h3>
<ul>
<li>When a device hears a carrier signal and transmits, a collision cannot occur.</li>
<li>A jamming signal causes only devices that caused the collision to execute a backoff algorithm.</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">All network devices must listen before transmitting.</span></li>
<li>Devices involved in a collision get priority to transmit after the backoff period.<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>Legacy bus-topology Ethernet LAN uses CSMA/CD as network media access control protocol. It works by detecting a collision in the medium and backing off (after transmitting a jam signal) as necessary. When one host wants to transmit a frame, it listens on the medium to check if the medium is busy. After it senses that no one else is transmitting, the host starts transmitting the frame, it also monitors the current level to detect a collision. If it detects a collision, it transmits a special jam signal so that all other hosts can know there was a collision. The other host will receive this jam signal and stop transmitting. After this, both hosts enter an exponential backoff phase and retry transmission.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>What is the auto-MDIX feature on a switch?</h3>
<ul>
<li>the automatic configuration of an interface for 10/100/1000 Mb/s operation</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">the automatic configuration of an interface for a straight-through or a crossover Ethernet cable connection</span></li>
<li>the automatic configuration of full-duplex operation over a single Ethernet copper or optical cable</li>
<li>the ability to turn a switch interface on or off accordingly if an active connection is detected<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The auto-MDIX enables a switch to use a crossover or a straight-through Ethernet cable to connect to a device regardless of the device on the other end of the connection.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<h3>Refer to the exhibit. What is the destination MAC address of the Ethernet frame as it leaves the web server if the final destination is PC1?</h3>
<figure id="attachment_211" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-211" style="width: 610px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-211" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20610%20355'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 4 – 7 Ethernet Concepts Exam Answers 03" width="610" height="355" data-lazy-srcset="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-4-–-7-Ethernet-Concepts-Exam-Answers-03.png 610w, https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-4-–-7-Ethernet-Concepts-Exam-Answers-03-300x175.png 300w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 610px) 100vw, 610px" data-lazy-src="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-4-–-7-Ethernet-Concepts-Exam-Answers-03.png" /><noscript><img decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-211" src="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-4-–-7-Ethernet-Concepts-Exam-Answers-03.png" alt="CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 4 – 7 Ethernet Concepts Exam Answers 03" width="610" height="355" srcset="https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-4-–-7-Ethernet-Concepts-Exam-Answers-03.png 610w, https://infraexam.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/CCNA1-v7-–-ITNv7-–-Modules-4-–-7-Ethernet-Concepts-Exam-Answers-03-300x175.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 610px) 100vw, 610px" /></noscript><figcaption id="caption-attachment-211" class="wp-caption-text">CCNA1 v7 – ITNv7 – Modules 4 – 7 Ethernet Concepts Exam Answers 03</figcaption></figure>
<ul>
<li>00-60-2F-3A-07-AA</li>
<li>00-60-2F-3A-07-BB</li>
<li><span style="color: #ff0000;">00-60-2F-3A-07-CC</span></li>
<li>00-60-2F-3A-07-DD<br />
<table>
<tbody>
<tr bgcolor="#e7f7e1">
<td>
<p><b>Answers Explanation &amp; Hints:</b></p>
<p>The destination MAC address is used for local delivery of Ethernet frames. The MAC (Layer 2) address changes at each network segment along the path. As the frame leaves the web server, it will be delivered by using the MAC address of the default gateway.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
